 <p data-pid="4w0lyPWt">眼瞅魁架就在跟前，再不搏就没机会了。小炮螳螂系紧安全带，一脚油门朝着左上方冲了上去。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8-oMZjU3">321、</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rlTwY2L-">能到留到最后的，必然不是莽夫。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SQWnTpkc">小炮螳螂这一下只是佯攻，途中提早收了速。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="eCeFHM5s">那舞狮尾的盲僧被这突如其来的冲击吓得一居灵，想都没想就是迎头一脚。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pdHLQr4E">小炮螳螂却是有心迎这一脚，暗中算计着角度。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ToczRaLt">被踢后，二人径直向右边飞去。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2P_930zS">322、</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dqC3ohSS">这一招可谓出其不意，可右边的老牛反应也是十分迅速。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PZ3-RWxv">一个半深蹲，架着牛角就迎面顶了过来。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NfUXJSDq">不料，小炮螳螂早埋好后手，双双一个横跳。反倒占到了上位。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RrCVzh6D">牛头扑了一个空，大骂一声，不好。却是为时晚矣。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2HfITL6o">323、</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="U3fLXu-l">那牛头皮糙肉厚，自是怕不得什么。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dsBAOomQ">可那老鼠就遭了殃，只得瑟瑟隐了身，大气不敢出。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VmzRRSkt">螳螂冷笑一声，使出虚空突刺，正中老鼠大腿。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FA3-QrPK">“gigigi”老鼠被刺得现了形，缠重难行。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="O2dgcp7J">324、</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="StX5tYRf">与其他的临时班子不一样，牛头老鼠可不是表面兄弟。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-O1AJGOd">见老鼠遭难，牛头想都不想就冲了上去，想用身体护住老鼠。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lej-K3_R">感人肺腑，却也只能是匹夫之勇。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="r7v-eRre">牛头匆匆赶过来，还未站稳脚跟，小炮一发炮弹，送两位兄弟双双把家还。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qrpD5aFf">325、</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ORfB26ZO">后面的路越来越滑，这么些个英雄要么身怀绝技，要么脚底板长得有爪子。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3Z_fdap4">但老子只穿了一双人字拖。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="r1sDkpBZ">不仅冷，抓地力实在太差了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="IhYHSOZP">我只能紧紧抱住阿狸，以防失足。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YlNrTdRF">可越往上，腿脚就越感觉蹬不上劲，我明显感觉到阿狸拖着我越来越吃力。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QP8gsKVH">326、</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-c9KqhJu">“老哥，你该减肥了！”阿狸转过头，报了之前调侃她的一箭之仇。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gdgct7MH">虽然这种挂在阿狸身上当累赘的感觉很美妙，但这毕竟不是旅行。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6uJyI-UN">果真打起来，我可不想成为一个蜷缩在角落瑟瑟发抖的OBC。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_yuq9Z6O">所以我打算去砍一些树枝，做一双雪地拐棍，两驱变四驱。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3XIt9JdX">327、</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KjOzZuWK">问题就出在这。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7ch8Lc0I">我发现我的西瓜刀抽不出来了！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ST0Y8_Ai">准确来说，温度太低导致西瓜刀的延展性出了问题，它盘在我的腰上，像一条冻僵的蛇。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VsCR9jn_">我一直对能喝上英雄醉深信不疑，现在我有一丝丝担忧。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bnbt1haq">328、</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fHhIOgbe">妈的，西瓜刀不能用，这不是明着削我么。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Xeead4w5">难道这召唤师峡谷里，冥冥之中自有平衡？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wVF4MpFa">刀不能用，我只得就近寻了一根粗树枝，用力踢断。由于不能处理细节，这根拐棍看上去实在过于抽象。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YH4e6GNh">枝干弯曲，复枝杂多，红色的叶子卤过的鸡爪。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EK4Rfint">拄着拐，怎么看怎么像一个过年时候，卖冰糖葫芦的。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gIE4w6sr">妈的，那又有什么办法呢？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jiZEBzvk">329、</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3nwQIJDD">螳螂小炮二人趁机加足马力，跃居到次席位置。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="o9ToHTPQ">排在最前面的是冰鸟努努，在冰冻的山路上，他俩有着得天独厚的优势。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1LdeHi0D">可此时，螳螂小炮二人信心膨胀得一p，眼瞅就到了魁架之下，岂有不争之理？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hNKLK_Ce">螳螂小炮一往无前，渐渐逼近排在最前面冰鸟努努。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2YALDvUB">330、</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9A9Q-g07">那领头的二人哪里肯依？</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WjJUawC-">努努趴在地上一顿鼓捣，搓出一个半人高的雪球来，对准螳螂小炮就推了下来。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="e45gOHcZ">这雪球的初速度不快，螳螂小炮稍稍一个横挪就躲了过去。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UJ0qACpR">可我们下面的队伍就没那么容易了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-EuZ1Vun">331、</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oSFku9F4">雪球越滚越大，越过越快。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="z2IsgMi_">在这陡滑的山上，雪球的威力大家可是都见识过的，稍有不慎就是一颗速冻肉丸。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GP4NHKdv">好在现在的队伍只剩下五只，彼此之间活动的空间还是挺富余的。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bma9W6ng">唯一受限的就是这陡滑的路面，谁都不敢做太夸张的动作。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="u-MtYifA">332、</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JCkjT3q8">泰坦看雪球滚下来，骂了一声，也算应付得从容。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="7e-mddEh">朝着侧面的石壁一钩子，便轻松带着盲僧躲到了石壁边。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vChnSDnp">可这盲僧不知是临时起了玩心，还是早生了恶意。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="z4358kyr">在雪球从他们一旁滚落下来时，这个家伙对着雪球狠狠踢了一脚。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EmnCkfuu">333、</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UrWy3HOM">这一脚真他喵的要命。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Cd4MKPrB">本来笔直滚落的雪球，现在以一个不规则的“S”形飞速滚下来。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kYVWstrv">这让雪球的路径极其不好预判，而且极大地减少了安全区域的面积。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DGhf-Ffl">所以必须要在极短的时间内作出反应。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fvCoVs9t">334、</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TMJQiWVa">霞洛，被誉为峡谷里的“神仙眷侣”。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cG6QSAN-">我一直觉得能配得上“神仙眷侣”之名的只可能存在于武侠小说里，诸如靖哥哥和蓉儿，以及杨过小龙女那般。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2nfAy9ug">雪球像一个醉驾的汽车，蛇形俯冲下来。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RTbY1nAi">洛二人身形娇小，必须很果断闪出雪球路径，否则就真的是冰雪过山车之情侣套餐了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bXmLMqH2">335、</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6-0xjB3Y">“走你~”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Tl71dzWu">只见洛竭力一推，将霞连同舞狮袍子一齐从侧面送到斜上方。而洛自己几乎是擦着雪球转身，赶紧往下跑。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wPX9gex4">“洛~洛~”霞在上面焦急地喊着洛的名字。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="-QYbc0Uj">“当危险来临，不经思考的奋不顾身，这就是爱情吧。”阿狸泛起花痴。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0N7WYil4">336、</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cn4XE3Ub">但起码我看到的，这不是一个悲伤的故事。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_LNU4dLe">洛这小子是真有俩下子，他趁着雪球在悬崖边折转抖起来的瞬间，一个漂亮的转身，从雪球下面滑过去。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1WtUcyH7">只不过这路太滑，洛一时没稳住重心，从悬崖边跌了出去。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BUY2VNz0">好在他情急之下抓紧了一根藤蔓，悬在了崖边。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="u-pAD1vI">337、</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="DN8cakkh">“把手给我，洛！”霞追跟着雪球一路赶下来，到底是虚惊一场。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hUxR7eTp">他俩套上舞狮袍，继续迈进，撒下一路狗粮。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pWXormUg">“看看，看看，互相扶持，这才是爱情。”我对阿狸说道。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Ovx1ag3D">“先别讨论这个，大雪球要来了。”阿狸直愣愣盯着前方。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xqKdD15z">338、</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TVuh3hAO">雪球滚下来，身形又胖了一圈。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="h3BGMKCl">我伸出手揉了揉腰，告诉她别慌，我数学老好了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="oKF-wR1g">6位数徒手开方都不怕，区区几何问题，无需多虑......</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="u0F8OTjp">雪球呼啸而过，我跟阿狸果然平安无事。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zuURBlO1">339、</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bqvWCknV">原理其实也挺简单，雪球近乎是一个球体，而山路的山壁一侧与山路呈一个直角。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wd6d-OBV">这球碰到直角就必然会有死角。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="1czNn6I9">所以只要待在这些死角里，就能保证安全。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YqvSE9M8">“这狗啃泥也算知识点？”阿狸白我一眼。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2oqKjOus">我跟阿狸从山墙角里爬起来，拍干净身上的冰渣子，也继续赶路去。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="bpaHnCBF">340、</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tZHCP3va">见这雪球贴近距离后不灵光了，螳螂小炮二人便越发膨胀起来。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dPj0npWI">明目张胆觊觎起领头狮的位置来。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mDMw-AH2">他们频频利用矫捷身手，从身后对冰鸟努努发起袭扰。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YAi0krYv">冰鸟努努二人受到袭扰，行径步态也跌跌撞撞起来。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="dAh7jhmj">341、</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="b-N8ajHG">努努干脆双手拽紧舞狮袍尾，身体半蹲，将大屁股朝后面撅起来，挡住了全部侵扰。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SavfmUOv">这螳螂小炮忙活了半天，才意识到——</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WFs_qbwa">这伤害全打到努努厚厚的脂肪上去了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xEAaoMwV">“看到那是什么了吗？”小炮问道。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SlaxX4P4">“屁股呀！”螳螂回道。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zbeiwFXY">342、</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5DU5_U6q">“错，那tmd是嘲讽。”小炮往炮筒猛灌了三倍的火药。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="rzNkjzvu">“我尼玛……”螳螂舔了舔锋利的爪子。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="XemlIsOB">这二人一对眼神，便一左一右冲了上去。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SyAKMbVc">这意图很明显——越过努努的大屁股，左右开弓打你家鸟。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="A-hpy_rE">343、</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WwK5YxKZ">努努弓着屁股，一时不知道该护住哪边。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RqVD8I9t">想着自己厚厚的脂肪，自是不怕物理伤害的。便摇晃着大屁股朝螳螂扑了过去。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="cL-jDCsa">这管一头，就顾不得另一头。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Fcrj8EwC">小炮拿着炮筒指着冰鸟，叫嚣道:</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mPPB1-Ee">“是自己回去，还是我帮你们？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="azZfdTSR">344、</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jsaZW8JL">冰鸟也不搭话。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0H8_zUBz">翅膀一挥，便拂去一股寒风。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="phim_Wla">小炮被冻得打了一个寒颤，骂道:</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5sCzcQa7">“真他娘的舒服，你还是下去卖冰阔落吧”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="K4W5_PtT">说罢，小炮恶狠狠扣动了炮机。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="WSqnFgS1">345、</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MLEHpmB1">boom！</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="by9rDJYD">炮筒炸膛，小炮送自己飞上了天。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JNTrgoRB">螳螂惊慌失措，拍着翅膀就要开遛。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8sYxuMV7">却是闷头撞到了坚硬的冰墙，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="O4PUoxO2">努努一发雪球送他入了地。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zTU8Qzkx">346、</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Z_uqzD4v">到了魁架之下，泱泱队伍只剩了四支。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ohte2dms">架高数米，四面呈梯。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="NACC0m7_">冰鸟努努二人的优势再无。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="kOBXCeyC">反倒是泰坦锤石如鱼得水，一钩子一个台阶。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zl2drhm9">347、</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4pNbyuOC">霞洛却是尤为不急，站在山顶说起了情话。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="meOut9t7">“快看呐洛，山顶真美”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="4WlgP_YE">“不如你美”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="q7NMMDxi">“噢，差点忘了”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wn_wVMkn">“我可一直都记着。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="l1ST3D55">348、</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3U_bpC-m">洛从怀中掏出照相机，走过来让我帮他们拍一张照。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ZHxEsfhf">“拍美一点”霞依偎在洛的怀里，脸上满是幸福。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="T2Kqm05H">这种直击心灵的美，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="O-XH4Gm1">把那那魁架上的争斗衬托得丑陋不堪。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="y2_gk1A4">349、</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="t_m5bUjp">“艹！我弄死你”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Z6cKZ63P">“艹，谁怕谁！”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="QUtFokNb">锤石与努努口吐芬芳起来。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="VWCxEigH">我顿然觉得什么英雄醉索然无味，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9dLoPHur">只觉得他们吵闹得不合时宜。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="H526vO4M">350、</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hqRS0G5z">等他们爬到了最上层，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lrmgnUu4">我掏出西瓜刀，开始砍魁架。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MHkg4ww1">一刀下去，摇摇欲坠。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zAZV6V5R">“艹，你弄啥呢？”他们骂道。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="YKGnxG2E">又一刀下去，魁架轰然倒塌，几个人拍落在地不省人事。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="TEKZFIh_">351、</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="Q8YeVeth">却是不留神，我叫坍塌的架子砸了。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9p9fDdgT">一阵剧痛让我跪到了地上。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="V5f7xk14">“伤哪里了？”阿狸焦急问道。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="PXajG_jk">我示意她不要大惊小怪，</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qwbQbta5">顿了顿，我扶着腰缓缓站了起来。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EDEOny6m">352、</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KV63dFDt">我让阿狸扶着我，从背面下了山。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EbAc7NQU">走了几十步，我打开衣服，发现腰椎红肿得厉害。阿狸捡了块冰给我敷上，问道:</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KiVL6cvs">“英雄醉不要了吗？”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="G5Qmousj">“不要了”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tBbgr_Nx">“那……下去怎么交代。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="d9k1FNv7">“交代个屁，输给爱情不丢人”</p>
</body>
